�� 3. Image Ad Breakdown – First Day IMAGE AD #3
: https://app.tryatria.com/ad/m3229668260499723

Core Psychological Principles at Play in the Image
System 1 Thinking (Fast, Emotional, Intuitive):
● Hook & Emotional Relevance: The giant, bold headline "ARE YOU ALWAYS SLEEPY?"
in all caps is a powerful System 1 hook. It bypasses rational thought and instantly
targets a visceral, common pain point. The viewer immediately self-identifies or ignores
the ad.
● Visual Pattern Interrupt: The bright yellow background is an aggressive scroll-stopper.
It acts as a visual jolt designed to grab attention.
● Processing Fluency (Visual): The layout is clean, text is high contrast, and emojis are
used to make the headline and key vitamin list extremely easy to understand. The brain
doesn’t have to work hard to comprehend it.
System 2 Thinking (Slow, Logical, Deliberative) – Initiated:
● Problem Framing & Explanation: The subheadline "3 vitamin deficiencies can create
chemical imbalances that may cause exhaustion" starts to engage System 2. It
introduces a plausible (though simplified) cause for the System 1 pain.
● Specificity & Credibility (Initial): Mentioning "Vitamin D," "Vitamin B12," and
"Magnesium" adds logic and specificity. This makes the problem and potential solution
feel more concrete.
● Product as Solution: A centered product image surrounded by healthy fruits/vegetables
builds the idea that this is a natural and credible remedy. System 1 says
"healthy/natural," while System 2 sees it as a formulated solution.

Zeigarnik Effect (Incompleteness & Curiosity):
● The headline "ARE YOU ALWAYS SLEEPY?" opens a mental loop: “Am I?” and “Why?” ●
The subheadline partially answers the why, and then the image implies the product is the
missing piece.
Loss Aversion (Implied):
● The phrase "ALWAYS SLEEPY" suggests loss of energy, productivity, and life
enjoyment. This taps into the discomfort of staying in a negative state.
Dopamine Spike (Novelty & Potential Reward):
● Bold question + bright color = pattern interrupt.
● The simple promise of a root cause and a possible fix (vitamin deficiencies + product)
triggers hope — a small dopamine hit.

How the Image Ad Works (Its Mechanism)
Interrupt & Qualify
● The headline and yellow background stop the scroll and quickly qualify the audience: “Is
this ad for me?”
Problem Agitation & Simplification
● It highlights a pain point (exhaustion) and immediately offers a simple explanation (3
vitamin deficiencies).
Introduce a Tangible Solution
● The product is presented in a clean, centered way with fresh foods implying health and
trust.
Prime for More Information
● The ad creates enough curiosity to make someone want to click. It gives a taste — not a
full picture.

Role in the Whole Funnel
Top of Funnel (TOF) – Primary Role
● Awareness & Attention: The ad grabs attention from tired people who may not know

why they feel that way.
● Problem Awareness/Education: It educates by introducing vitamin deficiency as a root
cause.
● Interest Generation: Curiosity is built toward the First Day product.
Early Middle of Funnel (MOF) – Secondary Role
● Solution Introduction: It positions First Day as a possible fix.
● Driving to Deeper Engagement: Encourages the user to click through to a landing
page for further logic-building (ingredients, proof, testimonials).

What the Image Ad Doesn't Do (and Isn’t Designed To):
● Deep System 2 Conviction: It only hints at a logical solution. Full persuasion is deferred
to the landing page.
● Overcome Major Skepticism: Lacks deep proof, testimonials, or detailed research.
● Social Proof: No review count, before/after, or community shown.
● Hard Sell/Direct Conversion: No price or CTA button. Implied CTA is "Learn More."

Conclusion
This image acts as a highly efficient scroll-stopper and problem-qualifier. It activates strong
System 1 triggers (emotion, visual impact) while lightly engaging System 2 with a simplified
logical narrative. Its ultimate goal is to move the viewer further into the funnel where deeper
persuasion happens.
LP: https://discover.firstday.com/wds-sales-exhaustion-lp
In summary:
The landing page is a logical and necessary continuation of the journey started by the static
image ad.
● The ad hooks them with a problem and a hint of a solution.
● The LP reels them in by confirming their problem, educating them thoroughly, building
overwhelming social proof, and making a compelling, risk-free offer.

�� 4. Ugly Image Ad Breakdown – IMAGE AD #4

: https://app.tryatria.com/ad/m560395226780496

Is This an "Ugly Image Ad"?
Yes – with caveats. It strongly leans into the psychology of ugly ads, though it’s not overtly low
quality or meme-like.
● Disrupts Pattern Recognition: The inflamed, textured red area on the body is visually
unsettling. Not a polished, lifestyle ad – it feels clinical or even alarming.
● Creates Novelty & Curiosity: The phrase "Cortisol Poisoning" is new and dramatic. The
unfamiliar visual invites inspection.
● Lowers Ad Defenses: Doesn’t feel like a traditional ad at first glance — more like a
medical infographic or warning. This bypasses ad fatigue.
● Feels "Real" or "Serious": The visual resembles something you’d see in a medical
presentation, creating urgency and realism.
What it’s NOT (Classic Ugly Ad Traits):
● Not pixelated, poorly cropped, or chaotic.
● No overuse of emojis or random overlays.
● Still structured and clean.
Conclusion: It employs ugly ad psychology — disruption, novelty, lowered defenses — with a
clinical/medical design twist. Less “chaotic meme,” more “diabolical infographic.”

Core Psychological Principles at Play in the Image & Copy
System 1 Thinking (Fast, Emotional, Intuitive)
● Hook & Emotional Relevance: "The Most Misunderstood Menopause Symptom:
Cortisol Poisoning" is dramatic, identity-targeted, and fear-inducing.
○ "Misunderstood" = intrigue, insider knowledge.
○ "Menopause Symptom" = demographic callout.
○ "Cortisol Poisoning" = invented fear trigger.
● Visual Alarm: The red inflamed spot evokes concern. Arrows amplify focus. Viewer
feels “this looks bad – what is it?”
● Fear-Based Copy:
○ "Cortisol might be eating your hip tendons like termites"
○ "Rogue hormone dismantling your body piece by piece"
○ "Silent collagen killer"
○ These phrases emotionally hijack the viewer’s attention and create urgency.
System 2 Thinking (Slow, Logical, Deliberative)
● Problem Framing & Pseudo-Scientific Justification: Reframes joint pain, fatigue,
aging skin as effects of a misunderstood cause ("Cortisol Poisoning").
● Borrowed Authority: Mentions studies from University of California, King’s College
London, UC San Diego — increases believability.
● Specificity in Copy:
○ "Reduce morning cortisol levels by 29%"
○ "Improved joint mobility by 41%"
○ These stats create perceived credibility and logic.
Zeigarnik Effect (Open Loop)
● Headline: "The Most Misunderstood Symptom..." prompts: “Why is it misunderstood?
What is cortisol poisoning?”
● Copy continues loop: “Doctors miss it 83% of the time.”
Loss Aversion (Dominant Principle)
● Visual: Red, inflamed organ suggests damage/loss.
● Copy: Drips with threats of ongoing or future loss:
○ "Sagging skin that ages 10 years"
○ "Radiating hip pain"
○ "Sleep disruption"
○ "Collagen breakdown"

○ "Mobility loss"
● Framing: If you don’t act now, you lose youth, comfort, beauty, sleep.
Anticipated Regret
● Narrative: Doctors miss this. If you ignore this now, you’ll regret it later.
● Implied Message: “What if your doctor is wrong?”
Dopamine Spike (Fear, Novelty, and Hope)
● Novelty: Unheard term “Cortisol Poisoning.”
● Fear/Surprise: Alarming symptoms.
● Hope: "Provitalize" = the natural solution that fixes everything.
Identity Trigger (Explicit)
● Copy: “Engineered specifically for women over 50 with hip and joint pain.”
● Clear callout of the exact avatar. Viewer feels: "They’re talking to me."

How the Image Ad Works (Its Mechanism)
Shock & Awe Hook
● Visual + term “Cortisol Poisoning” = Scroll-breaking.
● Feels urgent, unfamiliar, medical.
Problem Reframing & Amplification
● Takes familiar menopause symptoms and reframes them under a new, sinister lens. ●
Then heightens concern via extreme metaphors (“eating your tendons like termites”).
Undermines Existing Beliefs
● "Doctors miss it 83% of the time."
● "Your doctor won’t tell you this."
● "Big Pharma can’t patent natural solutions."
● Destroys trust in conventional wisdom, primes user to believe a new solution.
Introduce Secret Solution
● Provitalize is the answer.
● Framed as natural, safe, and science-backed.
Drive to Click

● Image is built to create discomfort and curiosity.
● Copy immediately delivers high agitation + solution, priming for a landing page visit.

Role in the Funnel
Top of Funnel (TOF)
● Purpose: Attention + curiosity + fear.
● Targets: Women 50+ with menopause-related pain/fatigue.
● Reframes: Offers a new way to view their symptoms.
MOF Transition Within Copy
● Copy immediately builds:
○ Product credibility (studies, natural ingredients).
○ Social proof (testimonials).
○ Offer and guarantee.
● Aims to accelerate from TOF to MOF conversion without leaving the ad.

Summary
This is a classic TOF “ugly ad” in disguise:
● Image = scroll-breaking, fear-inducing, curiosity-generating.
● Headline = massive open loop and identity trigger.
● Copy = mini-sales letter: problem agitation, skepticism toward mainstream, solution
intro, proof, and soft CTA.
● Designed for cold traffic and first contact — the image stops the scroll, the copy pulls
them into the story, and the link drives them to the BOF-heavy landing page for final
conversion.
LP: https://thebbco.com/pages/provitalize-j-gt-rpl

Is This an "Ugly Image Ad"?
Yes, absolutely. This is a textbook example of an “ugly image ad” that leans heavily on
psychology over aesthetics.
● Disrupts Pattern Recognition: A colorized X-ray with inflammation zones is stark and
diagnostic—not lifestyle or product-focused.
● Creates Novelty & Curiosity: "Chances are If It's not Arthritis It could Be Menopause"

Defenses: It resembles medical content, not a polished brand ad. This makes it feel more
informational and trustworthy.
● Feels Serious/Diagnostic: The medical design invokes concern and seriousness,
enhancing believability and urgency.

Core Psychological Principles at Play (Image + Copy)
System 1 Thinking (Fast, Emotional, Intuitive)
● Hook & Relevance:
○ X-ray evokes immediate concern.
○ Headline invalidates a common belief (arthritis) and introduces menopause—a
direct demographic callout.
● Visual Fear: Inflamed joint imagery = implicit health threat.
● Emotional Copy:
○ “I’m 47, in peri…”
○ “Throbbing pain returns.”
○ “Pain wakes me up.”

○ These lines instantly generate empathy and trigger concern.
System 2 Thinking (Slow, Logical, Deliberative)
● Problem Reframing: Shifts diagnosis from bursitis/arthritis to gluteal tendinopathy
caused by estrogen decline and gut issues.
● Scientific Framing: Mentions how estrogen affects tendons, how gut health links to

● Credibility Boosters:
○ Study references.
○ “90% of lateral hip pain” is due to this.
○ Trustpilot rating.

● Image Hook: “If It's not Arthritis It could Be Menopause” raises multiple questions.
● Copy reinforces loop with: “Does anyone else suffer the same?”, “Quick! Test
yourself…”, “Gluteal tendinopathy explained.”
Loss Aversion (Dominant)

● Copy:
○ "Suffering terribly."
○ "Couldn’t get up without wincing."
○ "Sleep destroyed."
○ “Menopause can make your joints feel like rusty hinges.”
○ “Tendon-deteriorating phenomenon.”
● Reader visualizes a worsening future if they don’t act.
Anticipated Regret
● Stories of failed treatments (physio, meds, misdiagnosis).
● “Don’t let hormonal joint aches get out of hand…” emphasizes urgency and
consequences of delay.
Narrative Transportation Theory
● Personal Story: Opens with a detailed first-person account of hip pain and struggle.
● Social Proof Layer: Adds “Sarah S.” and others’ transformation stories.
● Testimonials: Janet G., Kim H., Jennifer S., Donna T., etc. make it easy to identify with
others.

Social Proof & Bandwagon Bias
● "Over 2 Million Women Choose Provitalize" → now 3M+ in other versions.

Identity Trigger
● “I’m 47, in peri…”
● “Women’s joints in their 40s–60s…”

Pattern Interrupt & Intrigue
● X-ray = unusual, serious.

Problem Validation & Reframing

○ Explain cause + solution.

○ Offer.

�� 6. VSL Ad Breakdown – VSL AD #6 :
https://app.tryatria.com/ad/m469364065439704

Core Psychological Frameworks
System 1 & System 2 Thinking
● Hook (System 1): Rapid myth debunking – “Nope.” “That’s not it either.” Strong pattern
interrupt.
● Agitation (System 1): Security guard’s story: 12-hour shifts, pain, family life, emotional
cost.
● Mechanism (System 2): Dr. Campbell, calf pump mechanics, fluid pooling, valve
damage – backed by visuals.
● Solution (System 2): 3-in-1 device: compression + heat + massage. Mimics muscle
function to aid blood flow.
● Transformation (System 1 & 2): “Night and day difference,” “play with kids again,” “got
my life back.”
COM-B Model
● Capability: "15 minutes a day," "use it while watching TV." Passive and easy.
● Opportunity: Online purchase, 50% off, 90-day guarantee.
● Motivation: Built through frustration, pain, and transformation.
Self-Determination Theory
● Autonomy: Expert info + no-risk guarantee = viewer feels in control.
● Competence: Simple usage, feels achievable.

● Relatedness: Emotional story resonates deeply with target audience.
Narrative Transportation Theory
● Dominant Technique: Full ad is the narrator’s journey. Engaging from pain → solution
→ hope.
● Structure: Problem → Tension → Discovery → Solution → Result.
Loss Aversion
● Emphasizes what’s lost due to edema: life quality, energy, confidence, family moments.
Anticipated Regret
● Viewer sees ineffective paths, and is warned against continuing them. 90-day guarantee
removes fear.
Mirror Neurons & Identification
● Viewers easily see themselves in the narrator’s situation (especially people with
sedentary/standing jobs).
Processing Fluency
● Visual: Direct-to-camera + relatable footage + science animation + product in use.
● Verbal: Clear, structured explanation.
Anchoring
● Value: Dr. Campbell authority + mechanism = premium.
● Price: 50% off and 90-day guarantee anchors a great deal.
Pratfall Effect
● Narrator admits: “I was skeptical,” “Another gadget?” → builds credibility and trust.
Zeigarnik Effect (Open Loop)
● Myth busting + scientific curiosity → keeps viewer watching.
Social Proof & Bandwagon Bias
● Uses authority proof (Dr. Campbell) and deep first-person testimonial. ● Doesn’t
show multiple testimonials, but strong single-story + doctor credibility suffices.
Dopamine Spike

● Curiosity: Myth busting.
● Anticipation: Learning the hidden solution.
● Hope/Payoff: Transformation and offer.
Hook Psychology
● Contradiction/Myth Busting: “Nope.” “Wrong again.”
● Pain Mirror: Describes relatable life disruptions.
● Open Loop: Builds curiosity to uncover solution.

Funnel Placement
● TOF: Myth-busting, problem agitation.
● MOF: Deep product education, expert validation, logical persuasion.
● BOF: Offer (50% off), guarantee, CTA.
● Format: Full-Funnel VSL – educates, persuades, converts all in one asset.

Conclusion
This is a sophisticated VSL that utilizes multiple psychological levers to build belief and drive
conversions:
● Emotional hook + narrative-driven agitation
● Scientific explanation + expert authority
● Transformation + logical offer The VSL does nearly all the selling upfront,
pre-qualifying viewers with emotion and logic before pushing to the landing page. It's a
top-tier example of integrated full-funnel creative execution.

LP: https://try.nooro-us.com/review-40-3

Very simple to give you guys an example. Here goes back to OG Spencer cold calling days. Hey Jack, it's Spencer calling from EZA is now a bad time to talk. And you can obviously go ahead and schedule time to call them back. Or two, they'll just be like, no, I'm good, what's up? Right, and they'll probably answer because again, if you say that it's you like Spencer from EZA and they just purchased an order or it's Spencer from Aloe Yoga, they're probably, because they just placed an order, going to be like, oh, what's this about, right? So they'll be like, no, no, no, what's going on? And so if they do that, then you can say, I saw you just placed an order with us and I wanted to one, just personally reach out and thank you for supporting our brand. But two, I just wanted to ask if you could explain a little bit more about how you got to our brand, right? And you want to leave it there. You want to pause, you don't want to say anything else. You just want them to start talking about how they actually got to your brand. And if they ask like, oh, okay, like, what do you mean how I got to the brand? Then you can obviously explain a little bit further. Just be like, oh, I'm just looking to better understand like how'd you find out about us? Like, what were you looking for? Like, okay, well, what about our brand specifically? And you can just have a conversation but this is how you want to start it. BESTAND: 5.1 Understanding Your Product - Part 1.mp4
============================================================

All right, so in this next step here, or in this first step, what you're going to do is get a better understanding of your product, okay? Our ability to position your product in the market the right way is going to ultimately determine our success. If you're failing to create winning ads, it's because of three reasons. Number one, you do not understand where your product fits in the market. Number two, you don't understand what the market actually wants. Or number three, you are failing to execute, okay? And we're gonna get to the rest of that, but just know that understanding your product is the first and most important thing, because how the heck are you, you could understand what the market wants perfectly, but if you don't understand how your product fits in the market, you are not going to have success, okay? So what you're gonna want to do is you're gonna want to go into your self-onboarding questionnaire that you should have already filled out, and you're gonna take a look at some of the things that you wrote down, okay? So whatever your business differentiator is, make sure you start to jot those notes down, okay? FILE: Your ads depend on research quality not quantity.txt

---
title: "Your ads depend on research quality not quantity"
source: "https://www.skool.com/origins/quality-research"
author:
published:
created: 2026-06-28
description: "I could be wrong but this is something I've noticed that has produced better ads.  It doesn't matter if you spend 4 hours researching; you have to dig for gold."
tags:
  - "clippings"
---
[Archangel Luniw](https://www.skool.com/@archangel-luniw-1871?g=origins)

I could be wrong but this is something I've noticed that has produced better ads.

It doesn't matter if you spend 4 hours researching; you have to dig for gold. You could have 100 reddit quotes but if they're all like 20 upvote quotes, they won't mean anything because they aren't high resonant quotes.

You're probably on the right track if you've spent the last 3 hours researching and you barely have 2 pages because you're only copying comments and reddit quotes that have a hug upvote count and comment, or likes, that you also verify with other research.

This makes the ad creation process easier too. Like Schwartz says in BA, "You never create copy, you assemble it"

Hope this helps someone out there!

The best Stripe strategy is not a trick. It is running a real, compliant business.
Fast shipping. Great products. Clear communication. Elite customer service.

Stay compliant. Scale confidently. Lawyer up at $1M/month.

01 — THE COMPLIANCE-FIRST MINDSET
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Before you read a single word about Stripe setup, account creation, or scaling strategy, you need to
understand the single most important principle in this entire document: the best Stripe strategy is
staying compliant.
This is not about finding loopholes, gaming the system, or tricking risk analysts. Every strategy in
this guide is built on one foundation: running a real, legitimate business that Stripe genuinely wants
to keep on their platform. When you deliver great products fast, communicate clearly with customers,
and prevent chargebacks proactively, Stripe rewards you with smooth scaling, lower reserves, and
fewer reviews.

▶ The 6 Non-Negotiable Principles
#

PRINCIPLE

WHY IT MATTERS

1

Stay Compliant

Operate fully within Stripe's TOS. No prohibited products. No
misrepresentation. Compliance is not a burden — it is your shield.

2

Ship Fast

Speed kills chargebacks. When customers get their product quickly, they
do not dispute. Aim for delivery under 10 business days, ideally under 7.

3

Great Products

Sell products customers actually want and that match your descriptions.
Product quality directly reduces refunds, complaints, and disputes.

4

Clear Communication

Order confirmations, shipping updates, tracking emails, delivery
notifications. Customers who know what is happening do not panic and
chargeback.

5

Elite Customer Service

Respond under 24 hours. Resolve issues fast. Refund proactively when
warranted. Most chargebacks happen because customers could not reach
you.

Page 2

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

6

Chargeback Alerts

Ethoca, Verifi/CDRN, and Stripe Radar are not optional. They intercept
disputes before they hit your account. This is the #1 investment for
longevity.

COMPLIANCE IS NOT A LIMITATION. IT IS A COMPETITIVE ADVANTAGE.
Sellers who cut corners get shut down in months. Sellers who stay compliant run for years. Choose
your lane.

Everything in this guide flows from these six principles. The account setup is designed around
compliance. The review strategies are built on having genuinely good metrics. The scaling playbook
works because it is backed by real customer satisfaction. There are no tricks here — just the
framework for building a business that Stripe actively wants to support.

02 — PRE-SETUP FOUNDATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Before you create a Stripe account, your foundation needs to be rock solid. Rushing this step is the
number one reason accounts get flagged early. A proper foundation makes everything that follows
easier — reviews, scaling, and long-term account health.

▶ Business Entity & Legal Structure
Having a registered business entity (LLC, Ltd, Corporation, Sole Proprietorship) dramatically
increases your approval odds. Gather these before starting: business registration certificate, EIN or
tax ID, government-issued photo ID, a bank account in the business name, and proof of business
address.

⚡ Entity Matching

Your business name, address, and owner details must match EXACTLY across your Stripe
application, bank account, business registration, and website. Even small differences like "LLC" vs
"L.L.C." trigger manual review flags.

▶ Domain & Email Setup
Purchase your domain at least 2 weeks before applying. Set up professional email addresses on
your domain: support@yourbrand.com, info@yourbrand.com, and orders@yourbrand.com. Never
use Gmail or Yahoo for your Stripe business email. Domain age is a trust factor in Stripe's risk
scoring.
⚠ Domain Age Matters
A brand-new domain registered the same day as your Stripe application is one of the biggest red
flags in their automated system. Domains under 14 days old receive significantly higher risk scores.

Page 3

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

▶ Bank Account Preparation
Open a dedicated business bank account before applying. The account should have some
transaction history and a reasonable balance. Stripe may request bank statements during reviews,
and an active account with history looks far better than a freshly opened empty one. Make sure the
name matches your legal business name exactly.

▶ IP & Device Hygiene
Create and manage your Stripe account from a consistent, clean IP address. Your home or office
connection has the highest quality reputation. If you need a proxy, verify the IP quality at
scamalytics.com first. Low-quality IPs immediately elevate your risk score. Once your account is
created from a specific device and IP, continue managing from that same setup.

▶ Supplier & Product Preparation
Before you even apply to Stripe, make sure your product and supply chain are solid. You should
already have a reliable supplier with consistent quality, tested your products personally to verify
quality matches descriptions, established shipping times you can actually meet, and set up your
fulfillment pipeline so orders get processed quickly. This is not just about Stripe approval — it is
about running a business where customers are happy, products are good, and chargebacks never
happen in the first place.

03 — ACCOUNT CREATION MASTERCLASS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Every field on your Stripe application matters. Here is the exact walkthrough with the rationale
behind each choice.

▶ Step-by-Step Field Guide
FIELD

WHAT TO ENTER & WHY

Business Type

Select what matches your actual registration. LLC, Corporation, Sole
Proprietor, etc.

Legal Business Name

Exact registered name. Must match government docs and bank
account.

DBA / Brand Name

Your customer-facing brand name if different from legal name.

Business Phone

A real number where you can receive calls. Stripe may call for
verification. Consider a dedicated eSIM.

Business Address

Your registered address. Must match documents. PO Boxes
acceptable if registered.

Industry / MCC Code

Select the most accurate category for your actual products. Common:
Retail (general), Health & Beauty, Electronics, Home & Garden.

Business Website

Your fully built, policy-compliant, live store URL.

Page 4

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

▶ Product / Business Description
This is one of the most scrutinized fields. Write a clear, professional description covering what you
sell, who you sell to, how fulfillment works, and expected delivery times. Be specific. Be honest.

✅ STRONG DESCRIPTION:

"We are a B2C e-commerce brand specializing in [YOUR CATEGORY — e.g., health & beauty / fitness /
lifestyle / home goods]. We sell to customers primarily in [YOUR MARKETS — e.g., US, Canada, UK,
Australia]. Our product range includes [SPECIFIC PRODUCTS — e.g., skincare, supplements, resistance
bands, home fragrance]. All products are sold under our own brand [BRAND NAME], with custom
packaging, branded inserts, and quality-controlled inventory. Customers place orders through our website
[URL] and pay via credit card, Apple Pay, Shop Pay, and [OTHER METHODS]. Orders are processed and
shipped through our fulfillment partner within 24-48 hours, with average delivery times of 5-10 business
days. We maintain a dedicated customer service team with average response times under [X] hours. Our
brand has an active social media presence with [X,000+] followers across Instagram, TikTok, and
Twitter/X."

❌ WEAK DESCRIPTION:

"We sell products online. They ship from our suppliers to customers."

⚡ Customize EVERY Bracket

Replace every [BRACKET] with your actual data. The more specific and truthful you are, the stronger
your application. Stripe reviewers read thousands of these — specific details signal a real operation.
Vague descriptions signal a test account that will disappear in 30 days.

▶ Why Branding Changes Everything
This is the most overlooked advantage in e-commerce payment processing. When Stripe's risk team
reviews your account, they are asking one question: "Is this a real business or a fly-by-night
operation?" Nothing answers that question faster than visible branding. A branded business looks
permanent. An unbranded one looks disposable.
INVESTMENT

WHY IT MATTERS

Custom Packaging

Branded mailers, boxes, tissue paper, stickers, thank-you cards with
your logo. When a customer opens your package, it should feel like a
real brand — because it IS. This also generates unboxing content for
social media.

Branded Products

Private labeling or custom labels on your products. Even a simple
branded sticker on packaging transforms how customers AND
payment processors perceive your business.

Professional Product Photos

Real photos of YOUR actual products — not just supplier stock
images. Show them in branded packaging. Show lifestyle shots. Show
them in use. This is evidence for Stripe AND conversion optimization
for your store.

Brand Inserts

Business cards, discount cards, QR codes linking to your socials,
thank-you notes inside every package. These cost pennies and create
a premium brand experience.

Page 5

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Branded Website

Consistent colors, fonts, logo placement, professional "About Us"
story. Your website should look like a brand someone spent time
building — not a template thrown up overnight.

▶ Invest in Real Stock
Holding real inventory — even small quantities — is one of the strongest signals you can send to
any payment processor. It proves you are a real operation with real money invested, not a
middleman forwarding orders from AliExpress. The moment you invest in stock, you go from
"random dropshipper" to "real brand with skin in the game."

☑ Start with a small stock order (50-200 units) of your best sellers
☑ Take photos of YOUR inventory — stacked, organized, labeled with your branding
☑ Keep purchase invoices from your supplier as proof of investment
☑ Use a 3PL (third-party logistics) warehouse if you cannot store inventory yourself
☑ Re-order before you run out — consistent stock availability = consistent fulfillment = no delays
☑ Supplier agreements on official letterhead prove ongoing business relationships
☑ Save warehouse photos, packing station photos, shipping label photos — all future review
evidence

✅ Stock + Branding = Trust Shield

When a Stripe reviewer sees branded product photos, professional packaging shots, and supplier
invoices, your account stops looking like a risk and starts looking like an asset they want to keep.
This is the single highest-ROI investment you can make for account longevity.

▶ Social Media Presence as Legitimacy Proof
An active social media presence is no longer optional. It is a trust signal that payment processors,
customers, and even banks evaluate. A business with 10,000+ real followers on Instagram, content
on TikTok, and engagement on Twitter/X looks fundamentally different to a risk analyst than a
business with zero online presence.
PLATFORM

HOW TO USE IT

Instagram

Post product photos, customer reviews, behind-the-scenes content,
packaging videos. Aim for consistency (3-5 posts/week). Followers
and engagement prove you are a real, active brand.

TikTok

Product demos, unboxing videos, trending sounds with your products.
TikTok can explode your brand awareness AND serves as proof of
legitimacy for processors.

Twitter / X

Brand updates, customer interactions, industry engagement. Your
@handle becomes part of your professional identity that you
reference in review responses.

Page 6

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

YouTube

Product reviews, tutorials, brand story content. Long-form content
signals serious investment in your brand.

Trustpilot / Reviews

Actively collect customer reviews on Trustpilot, Google Reviews, or
your own site. A 4.5+ star rating with real reviews is powerful
evidence during any hold or review.

Your social media is not just marketing. It is documentation. Every post, every follower, every
positive comment is evidence that you are building something real. When you eventually face a
review or hold, you will screenshot your profiles and attach them as proof of business legitimacy.
Start building now, not when you need it.

⚠ Social Media = Leverage in Disputes
Beyond legitimacy proof, your social media following becomes direct leverage if you ever face an
unjustified hold or termination. A brand with 50,000 followers saying "We will share our experience
publicly" carries real weight with risk teams. You are not just building a marketing channel — you are
building insurance.

▶ Statement Descriptor
This is what appears on your customer's bank statement. Use your brand name or a clear
abbreviation. If customers do not recognize the charge, they chargeback. This single field directly
impacts your dispute rate.
ELEMENT

DETAILS

Good Descriptors

YOURBRAND.COM, YOURBRAND, YOURBRAND*ORDER

Bad Descriptors

STRIPE*, PYMNT, random abbreviations customers will not recognize

Max Length

22 characters. Keep it clear, recognizable, and consistent.

▶ Fulfillment & Shipping Details
FIELD

RECOMMENDED

Fulfillment Method

Shipped by third-party / Shipped from warehouse (whichever is
accurate)

Shipping Time

Be honest and realistic. "7-14 business days" international. "3-7"
domestic.

Return/Refund Policy

Clearly state your refund window (14-30 days recommended) and
process.

Stripe checks whether your stated shipping times match reality. If you say 5-10 days but customers
regularly wait 20+ days, that mismatch creates chargebacks and flags your account. Underpromise
and overdeliver. Always.

▶ Security Setup

Page 7

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Enable two-factor authentication immediately. Use an authenticator app (Google Authenticator,
Authy, 1Password) rather than SMS. Save backup codes securely. 2FA strengthens your account's
trust profile and protects against unauthorized access.

04 — WEBSITE & STOREFRONT REQUIREMENTS
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Your website is the first thing Stripe reviews and it gets re-scanned during every subsequent review.
A professional, policy-compliant website is non-negotiable. It also directly impacts customer trust,
which means fewer chargebacks.

▶ Mandatory Website Elements
☑ Clear product listings with real images, accurate descriptions, and honest pricing
☑ Visible business name, address, and contact information in the footer of every page
☑ Working contact email AND phone number on a dedicated Contact Us page
☑ Comprehensive Refund & Return Policy (specific to your business, not a generic template)
☑ Shipping Policy with estimated delivery times by region
☑ Privacy Policy page (customized with your actual business details)
☑ Terms of Service / Terms & Conditions page
☑ Active SSL certificate (HTTPS)
☑ Professional domain-based email displayed (support@yourbrand.com)
☑ About Us page establishing your brand story and legitimacy
☑ Order tracking page or tracking link in order confirmation emails
⚠ No Generic Policy Templates
Stripe reviewers and customers can both spot cookie-cutter policies instantly. Customize every policy
page with your actual business name, real contact details, specific return windows, accurate shipping
information, and your actual refund process. Generic policies signal an unprofessional operation.

▶ Communication Touchpoints on Your Website
Clear communication starts on your website. Customers should never have to guess when their
order will arrive, how to contact you, or what your refund process is. Every piece of information they
need should be visible and easy to find. This transparency directly prevents chargebacks from
confused or frustrated customers.

☑ Shipping timeline clearly displayed on every product page (not just the shipping policy page)
☑ Expected delivery date shown at checkout before the customer pays
☑ Multiple ways to contact support visible on every page (email, phone, live chat)
☑ FAQ page addressing common questions about shipping, returns, and product details
☑ Order tracking accessible directly from your website (not just via email)

Page 8

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

05 — THE 5 PILLARS OF ACCOUNT SURVIVAL
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Your Stripe account lives or dies based on five operational pillars. Master all five and your account
will run for years with minimal friction. Neglect any one of them and you are on borrowed time.
These are not suggestions — they are survival requirements.

▶ Pillar 1: Fast Shipping
Shipping speed is the single biggest controllable factor in preventing chargebacks. The longer a
customer waits for their product, the more likely they are to panic, lose patience, and file a dispute.
Fast shipping eliminates this risk almost entirely.
SPEED TIER

IMPACT

Gold Standard

Under 7 business days from order to delivery. Customers are thrilled,
disputes are near zero.

Acceptable

7-12 business days. Most customers are patient. Clear
communication keeps disputes low.

Risky

12-18 business days. Disputes start climbing. Requires excellent
communication to manage.

Account Killer

18+ business days regularly. Chargeback rates spike. Stripe will
intervene.

☑ Use the fastest fulfillment option you can afford for your margins
☑ Upload tracking numbers to every order within 24 hours of shipment
☑ Use trackable carriers that provide delivery confirmation (USPS, UPS, FedEx, DHL, etc.)
☑ Set shipping expectations honestly on product pages and at checkout
☑ If a shipment is delayed, proactively email the customer BEFORE they have to ask

✅ Speed = Trust = Zero Chargebacks

A customer who receives their product in 5 days has almost zero reason to dispute the charge. A
customer waiting 25 days with no updates has every reason. Invest in shipping speed. It is the
highest-ROI investment in your entire operation.

▶ Pillar 2: Elite Customer Service
Most chargebacks do not happen because the product is bad. They happen because the customer
could not reach anyone to resolve their issue. If you respond fast, resolve problems generously, and
make customers feel heard, they will contact you instead of their bank. That is the entire game.
ELEMENT

STANDARD

Response Time

Under 24 hours mandatory. Under 6 hours ideal. Under 2 hours is
world-class and virtually eliminates disputes.

Channels

Email at minimum. Live chat is a massive upgrade. Phone support for
high-volume operations.

Page 9

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Refund Policy

Be generous. A $30 refund costs you $30. A lost chargeback costs
$30 + $15 fee + damage to your dispute rate.

Resolution Authority

CS team should have authority to refund, reship, or offer discounts
without escalation. Speed of resolution matters.

Proactive Outreach

If you know a shipment is delayed, contact the customer FIRST.
Proactive communication prevents 90% of disputes.

⚠ The Refund-First Philosophy
It is almost ALWAYS cheaper to refund a customer than to fight a chargeback. A refund costs you the
transaction amount. A lost chargeback costs the transaction amount PLUS a $15 dispute fee PLUS
lasting damage to your dispute rate metric. Build a culture where your team refunds generously and
quickly. Your Stripe account will thank you.

▶ Pillar 3: Product Quality
Selling products that match their descriptions and meet customer expectations is not just good ethics
— it is chargeback prevention. When the product a customer receives looks like what they ordered,
works as described, and feels worth the price, disputes simply do not happen.

☑ Order samples of every product BEFORE listing it. Verify quality matches your descriptions.
☑ Use real product photos (not just supplier stock images) whenever possible
☑ Write honest, specific product descriptions. Overblown marketing creates expectations
products cannot meet.
☑ Include accurate sizing, dimensions, materials, and weight on every product page
☑ If a product has known limitations, mention them. Honest descriptions prevent returns.
☑ Monitor product reviews and customer feedback. If multiple people report the same issue, fix
or remove the product.
☑ Maintain relationships with suppliers who consistently deliver quality. Replace unreliable
suppliers immediately.

⚡ The Quality-Description Match

The gap between what your product page promises and what the customer receives is directly
proportional to your chargeback rate. Close that gap to zero and your dispute rate follows.

▶ Pillar 4: Clear Communication at Every Step
Customers who know exactly what is happening with their order do not chargeback. Silence is what
creates panic, frustration, and disputes. Build an automated communication system that keeps
customers informed at every stage of the journey.
STAGE

WHAT THE CUSTOMER RECEIVES

Order Confirmation

Immediate email: "We received your order! Here is what you bought
and your expected delivery date."

Processing Update

Within 24 hours: "Your order is being prepared for shipment."

Page 10

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Shipping Notification

When shipped: "Your order is on the way! Here is your tracking
number: [LINK]"

In-Transit Updates

Automated tracking updates via email or SMS as the package moves.

Delivery Confirmation

When delivered: "Your order has been delivered! We hope you love it.
Contact us if you need anything."

Follow-Up

3-5 days post-delivery: "How is your product? Leave a review or let us
know if we can help."

Use Shopify's built-in email notifications, or upgrade to tools like Klaviyo, Omnisend, or AfterShip for
richer automated communication flows. The goal is that a customer never has to ask "Where is my
order?" because they already know.

▶ Pillar 5: Chargeback Alert Systems
Chargeback alerts are the most important defensive tool in your entire stack. These services
intercept disputes BEFORE they become chargebacks on your Stripe account. When a customer
initiates a dispute with their bank, the alert service notifies you first, giving you the chance to refund
the transaction and prevent the chargeback from ever hitting your record.
TOOL

WHAT IT DOES

Ethoca Alerts

Intercepts disputes from Mastercard transactions. Notifies you to
refund before the chargeback is filed.

Verifi / CDRN

Intercepts disputes from Visa transactions. Same concept: early
warning to refund proactively.

Stripe Radar

Stripe's built-in fraud detection. Enable it, configure custom rules, and
enable 3D Secure on flagged transactions.

Chargeback Guaranty

Services like Chargeflow, Disputifier, or Midigator that automate
dispute responses and sometimes guarantee wins.

CHARGEBACK ALERTS ARE NOT OPTIONAL. THEY ARE MANDATORY.
Ethoca + Verifi cover Mastercard + Visa. Stripe Radar covers fraud. Together they catch 80%+ of
potential chargebacks before they hit your account. The cost is negligible compared to the account
protection they provide.

☑ Enroll in Ethoca Alerts immediately after account creation
☑ Enroll in Verifi / CDRN for Visa-side coverage
☑ Enable Stripe Radar and configure custom rules for your product category
☑ Enable 3D Secure on transactions flagged as medium-to-high risk
☑ Set up webhook alerts in Stripe for instant dispute notifications
☑ When you receive a chargeback alert, refund the transaction IMMEDIATELY — do not wait

Page 11

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

☑ Monitor your dispute rate daily through the Stripe Dashboard
☑ If dispute rate approaches 0.5%, pause scaling and address root causes immediately

06 — CHARGEBACK PREVENTION & ALERT SYSTEM
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Your dispute rate is the single most important metric for your Stripe account's survival. Stripe's
published threshold is 0.75% but you should operate well under 0.5% at all times. This section builds
a complete, layered prevention system.

▶ Layer 1: Pre-Purchase Prevention
☑ Accurate product descriptions and real photos that match what customers receive
☑ Clear, prominent shipping timeframes on product pages AND at checkout
☑ Easily visible and understandable refund/return policy
☑ Statement descriptor customers will recognize on their bank statement
☑ Stripe Radar fraud detection enabled with custom rules
☑ 3D Secure authentication on high-risk transactions
☑ Address verification (AVS) and CVC checks enabled
▶ Layer 2: Post-Purchase Prevention
☑ Immediate order confirmation email with expected delivery date
☑ Proactive shipping updates with live tracking link
☑ Easy-to-find customer support contact on all emails and your website
☑ Rapid CS response time (under 24 hours, ideally under 6)
☑ Generous refund policy — cheaper to refund than to fight a chargeback every time
☑ Post-delivery follow-up email asking about satisfaction
▶ Layer 3: Active Interception
☑ Ethoca Alerts enrolled and monitored for Mastercard dispute interception
☑ Verifi / CDRN enrolled and monitored for Visa dispute interception
☑ Instant refund upon chargeback alert — never let an alert convert to an actual chargeback
☑ Stripe webhook alerts configured for real-time dispute notifications
☑ Daily dispute rate monitoring through Stripe Dashboard
☑ Monthly analysis of dispute reasons to identify and fix root causes
☑ If dispute rate hits 0.5%, STOP scaling and fix the problem before continuing
▶ Layer 4: Dispute Response (When Prevention Fails)
Even with perfect prevention, some chargebacks will come through. When they do, respond with
overwhelming evidence within the deadline. Include: order confirmation, shipping confirmation with
tracking, delivery confirmation, product photos, customer communication logs, and your refund
policy. Stripe provides a response interface in the Dashboard for each dispute.

Page 12

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

07 — SECURITY & VERIFICATION
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Identity verification is the most critical milestone for your Stripe account. Until this is passed, your
account is provisional. Do not scale until verification is complete.

▶ Verification Best Practices
☑ Have government-issued photo ID ready (passport preferred for clarity)
☑ Ensure good lighting and clean background for verification photos
☑ Complete verification from the SAME IP region where your account is managed
☑ If the representative is elsewhere, they must use a connection from the same region
☑ Complete verification promptly when requested — delays increase risk scores
☑ Never attempt verification from a different country than your account management location
⚠ Location Mismatch = Account Death
If your Stripe account is managed from Country A but verification is completed from Country B
thousands of miles away, this creates an extreme risk flag. This single issue causes a massive
percentage of early terminations. Ensure geographic consistency at all times.

08 — THE REVIEW GAUNTLET
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

As volume grows, Stripe conducts increasingly thorough reviews. When your compliance, shipping,
product quality, customer service, and chargeback prevention are all dialed in, reviews become easy.
You are not making up stories — you are reporting facts.

▶ Review Stage Map
STAGE

TRIGGER

RISK

WHAT THEY ASK

ID Verify

First few sales

⚠ HIGH

Government ID, selfie, address

Review #1

$1-3K/day

⚠ HIGH

Business model, chargebacks,
processing history, bank statements

Review #2

$5-10K/day

⚠ MEDIUM

Business liquidity, funding, supplier
relationships

Review #3+

$15K+/day

ℹ LOW-MED

Ongoing compliance, updated financials,
volume justification

▶ First Business Review — The Critical One

Page 13

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

This review triggers around $1,000-$3,000/day. Stripe wants to understand your business model,
how you handle chargebacks, and whether you are a real operation. When you have genuinely good
metrics, real stock, fast shipping, and active chargeback prevention tools, this review becomes
straightforward.
What Makes a Winning Review Response

☑ Detailed business model description with specifics on products, markets, and fulfillment
☑ Honest chargeback data with your actual low dispute rate as proof
☑ Chargeback prevention tools listed: Ethoca, Verifi, Stripe Radar, 3D Secure all enrolled
☑ Customer service metrics: response time, resolution rate, satisfaction score
☑ Fast shipping proof: average fulfillment time, average delivery time, tracking upload rate
☑ Bank statements showing healthy balances and business activity
☑ Processing history from other platforms showing clean track record
☑ Supplier agreements and stock photos proving real inventory

✅ When Compliance Makes Reviews Easy

If your dispute rate is genuinely 0.2%, your average delivery time is 7 days, your CS response time is
4 hours, and you have Ethoca + Verifi enrolled — just report those facts. You do not need to spin or
embellish. The truth is the most compelling evidence. This is why compliance-first is the strategy.

▶ Second Business Review
This review focuses on financial health and business stability. Be prepared to discuss funding
access, credit facilities, cash reserves, supplier payment terms, and overall capitalization. Answer
confidently and back everything with documentation.

▶ Review Response Template
When responding to any review, use this structure for your business description:

✅ STRONG REVIEW RESPONSE:

"We are [BRAND NAME], a branded e-commerce company selling [CATEGORY] products B2C to
customers in [COUNTRIES]. Products include [SPECIFICS], all sold under our own brand with custom
packaging and branded inserts. Customers order through our webshop [URL] using [PAYMENT
METHODS]. Our fulfillment partner processes orders within 24 hours and ships via [CARRIERS]. Average
delivery time is [X] days. We maintain a dispute rate of [X.XX]% with Ethoca and Verifi chargeback alert
services enrolled. Our customer service team responds within [X] hours on average. We have [X] months
of clean processing history and an active social media presence with [X,000+] followers across Instagram
(@HANDLE), TikTok, and Twitter/X."

❌ WEAK REVIEW RESPONSE:

"We sell stuff online and ship it to customers. We don't really have chargebacks."

09 — SCALING PLAYBOOK
Page 14

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Scaling safely requires discipline, consistency, and the operational foundation you have been
building. When your shipping is fast, your CS is elite, your products are solid, and your chargeback
alerts are active, scaling is just a matter of gradually increasing volume while maintaining those
standards.

▶ The Golden Scaling Rule

Scale as fast as your metrics allow. If dispute rate, shipping, and CS hold
steady — keep pushing.
The only speed limit is your operational quality. If your 5 pillars are green, scale aggressively. If
anything slips, pause and fix before continuing.

▶ Volume Progression Timeline
TIMELINE

VOLUME & FOCUS

Day 1-3

$0 – $1,000/day: First sales. Trigger ID verification. Confirm fulfillment
pipeline is working. Upload tracking on every order from day one.

Week 1-2

$1,000 – $3,000/day: Build initial processing history. Prove fast
shipping. CS locked in under 24hr. Monitor dispute rate daily. Have
review docs ready.

Week 3-4

$3,000 – $7,000/day: First review zone. Submit your real metrics
confidently. Branded stock photos, supplier agreements, and tracking
exports ready to go.

Week 5-8

$7,000 – $15,000/day: Post-review scaling. If reserve applied,
negotiate down after 30 days (see Section 10). Maintain all 5 pillars.
Hire CS if needed.

Month 3-4

$15,000 – $30,000/day: Second review zone. Prove liquidity. Show
consistent growth with stable dispute rate. Bank statements showing
healthy balances.

Month 4-6

$30,000 – $50,000+/day: Mature operation. Reviews become routine.
Start planning for the $1M/month milestone and lawyer up (see
Section 11). Consider backup processor.

▶ Scaling Safety Metrics to Monitor Daily
☑ Dispute rate: keep under 0.5% at all times. Below 0.3% is excellent.
☑ Refund rate: keep consistent and reasonable. Sudden spikes are flagged.
☑ Average delivery time: maintain or improve as volume increases. Never let it slip.
☑ CS response time: maintain under 24 hours regardless of volume. Hire if needed.
☑ Tracking upload rate: 100% of orders, no exceptions.
☑ Chargeback alert response time: refund within hours of receiving an alert, not days.
☑ Product return rate: monitor for quality issues. If returns spike on a product, investigate
immediately.

Page 15

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

⚠ Scaling Without Quality = Death
Scaling volume while customer service degrades, shipping slows down, or product quality drops is
the fastest way to kill your account. Every time you increase volume, verify that all 5 pillars (shipping,
CS, product quality, communication, chargeback alerts) are maintaining their standards. If any pillar is
slipping, fix it BEFORE scaling further.

10 — RESERVE & HOLD MANAGEMENT
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

After business reviews, Stripe may apply a reserve (typically 25% held for 90-120 days). This is
standard and manageable. Reserves can almost always be negotiated down, especially when your
metrics genuinely support it.

▶ Reserve Types
TYPE

DESCRIPTION

Rolling Reserve

Percentage of each payout held for a set period (e.g., 25% for 90
days, released on rolling basis)

Fixed Reserve

Lump sum held that does not change with volume

Payout Delay

Payout schedule extended (e.g., from 2 days to 7 or 14 days)

▶ Negotiating Reserves Down
Wait at least 30 days of clean processing, then contact Stripe with a data-backed request. When
your chargeback alerts are enrolled, your dispute rate is low, your shipping is fast, and your CS is
responsive, the data speaks for itself.

☑ Wait 30-60 days to build a clean track record since the reserve was applied
☑ Document dispute rate consistently below 0.5% during the period
☑ Show Ethoca and Verifi enrollment as active chargeback prevention
☑ Provide bank statements showing healthy balances
☑ Include tracking data showing fast delivery times and high confirmation rates
☑ Present customer service metrics (response time, resolution rate)
☑ Contact Stripe with a formal, evidence-based request to reduce to 10% or remove entirely
☑ If denied, wait 30 days with updated data and try again. Persistence works.

11 — THE $1M/MONTH MILESTONE
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Page 16

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Hitting $1 million per month in processing volume is a major business milestone. At this scale, you
are running a serious operation with significant financial exposure. This is when you need to level up
your infrastructure beyond what got you here.

▶ Why $1M/Month = Lawyer Up

AT $1M/MONTH: GET A PAYMENTS ATTORNEY ON RETAINER.
This is not optional. This is a business-critical investment.

At $1 million per month, the stakes are too high to navigate payment processing disputes, holds, or
compliance issues without legal representation. A payments attorney protects your operation in ways
that no amount of DIY effort can match.

▶ What a Payments Attorney Does for You
SERVICE

WHY IT MATTERS AT $1M+

Hold & Reserve Response

Attorney-drafted responses to holds carry 10x more weight than
self-written emails. Risk teams treat legal letterhead differently.

Contract Review

Review your Stripe agreement, supplier contracts, and fulfillment
agreements to identify and close liability gaps.

Compliance Audit

Proactively review your operations for compliance risks before Stripe
or regulators find them.

Regulatory Protection

Navigate PCI DSS, consumer protection laws, cross-border
regulations, and card network rules.

Dispute Escalation

When standard channels fail, your attorney can file formal legal
demands that accelerate resolution.

Business Structure

Advise on entity structure, asset protection, and liability separation as
your revenue scales.

Processor Negotiation

Negotiate better processing rates, lower reserve requirements, and
more favorable terms at scale.

▶ Finding the Right Attorney
☑ Look for attorneys specializing in payments law, e-commerce law, or fintech law
☑ They should have experience with Stripe, PayPal, and Shopify Payments specifically
☑ Ask for references from other e-commerce businesses they represent
☑ Expect to pay $2,000-$5,000/month for a retainer at this level — it is worth every dollar
☑ The attorney should be able to draft demand letters, review processor agreements, and
handle regulatory issues
☑ Consider firms that specialize in merchant services: they know the industry and the players

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

⚡ The ROI of Legal Representation

At $1M/month, even a single 5-day payout hold costs you significant operational disruption. A
payments attorney on retainer can often resolve holds in 48-72 hours with a single demand letter.
The $3,000/month retainer pays for itself the first time it saves a $30,000+ hold from dragging on for
weeks.

▶ Other $1M/Month Upgrades
At this volume, also invest in these infrastructure upgrades:

☑ Dedicated accountant or CFO-level financial management
☑ Business insurance including product liability and cyber liability coverage
☑ Dedicated fraud analyst or fraud prevention service beyond Stripe Radar
☑ Backup payment processor (Adyen, Checkout.com, or similar) in case of Stripe issues
☑ Enterprise-grade chargeback management platform with automated responses
☑ Formal supplier agreements reviewed by your attorney with liability protections
☑ Business banking relationship manager for faster financial operations

12 — LONG-TERM ACCOUNT HEALTH
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Maintaining a healthy Stripe account is an ongoing discipline, not a one-time setup. The habits you
build in the first few months determine whether your account lasts for years. Consistency in
compliance, service, and quality is what separates lasting businesses from flash-in-the-pan
operations.

▶ Monthly Maintenance Checklist
☑ Review dispute rate — ensure consistently below 0.5%
☑ Verify chargeback alert services (Ethoca, Verifi) are active and responding
☑ Update business profile if anything has changed (products, address, volume expectations)
☑ Ensure website policies are current, accurate, and match your actual operations
☑ Verify CS team is meeting response time targets (under 24hr, ideally under 6hr)
☑ Review shipping performance — are delivery times meeting or exceeding promises?
☑ Check product quality feedback — address any recurring complaints immediately
☑ Optimize Stripe Radar rules based on recent fraud patterns
☑ Ensure statement descriptors are still accurate for current product mix
☑ Keep all business documentation current and ready for potential reviews
☑ Monitor and improve customer communication automations
☑ Review refund reasons for patterns that indicate product or description issues
▶ Red Flags That Kill Accounts
RED FLAG

WHY IT KILLS YOUR ACCOUNT

Page 18

STRIPE & PAYMENT PROCESSOR GUIDELINES

Dispute rate > 0.75%

Stripe's published threshold. Above this, expect immediate action.
Card networks enforce at 1%.

Sudden volume spikes

More than 2-3x normal volume without gradual buildup triggers
automated holds.

Declining CS quality

Slower response times as you scale = more chargebacks. Hire before
you need to.

Product quality drops

Switching to cheaper suppliers saves money short-term, kills
accounts long-term.

Shipping delays

If average delivery time is creeping up, customers are getting
frustrated and disputing.

Stale chargeback alerts

Ethoca/Verifi enrolled but not being monitored or acted on defeats the
entire purpose.

Ignoring review requests

Failing to respond promptly to Stripe reviews is an immediate red flag.

Policy pages outdated

Policies that do not match your current operations create compliance
risk.

SHIP FAST. SERVE BETTER. SELL QUALITY. COMMUNICATE CLEARLY.
Enroll in chargeback alerts. Stay compliant. Lawyer up at $1M/month.
The best Stripe account strategy is running a business Stripe wants to keep.
